<section type="Title-page">
THE
HERBALL
OR GENERALL
Historie of 
Plantes.

Gathered by Iohn Gerarde
of London Master in
CHIRVRGERIE

Very much
Enlarged and Amended by
Thomas Johnson
Citizen and Apothecarye
of
LONDON

London Printed by
Adam Islip Ioice Norton
and Richard Whitakers
<term lang="la">Anno</term> 1633.
</section>
